Hi Niksan,   
  
these are added manually to the chart using the edit chart options in MT4. If you haven't got them click on View, Toolbars, Linestudies to add the toolbar to your Mt4. Now you should have access to all the options, right click on the line studies, customise and you can add or remove the buttons you want to see and use. Add Arrows to your line studies toolbar.  
  
J

  * [#408](/thread/post/4657052#post4657052 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 1, 2011 9:01am  Jun 1, 2011 9:01am 

  * [ julie1585](julie1585)

  * | Joined Oct 2009  | Status: Trader | [150 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=118395)

> [Quoting Ridgeback](/thread/post/4655861#post4655861 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> thanks for your reply.  
>    
>  What settings do you use on TzPivotsD? Do you leave it at GMT +0?  
>  If I do I get quite different pivot points compared to   
>  [http://www.actionforex.com/markets/p...2010040873429/](http://www.actionforex.com/markets/pivot-points/gbp%10usd-pivot-points-2010040873429/)  
>    
>  Ridge
> 
> Ignored

check you have changed it to DPV (Daily Pivots) and not using default FPV, (Fibonacci Pivots) should have 1 in the box not 2, and yes I leave GMT at 0.   
  
For me having 0 GMT means the new day starts at beginning of Asian session, being Australian that works fine for me, I have noticed the pivots used on other websites do differ, not gone into it much as I can see my daily pivot is recognised by price action. For example right at this moment gbpusd is finding resistance at DPV, so even if the real daily pivot for the rest of the world is something else, price is still recognising this pivot. I don't like getting too bogged down on the whys and wherefores, you would have to go study pivots elsewhere to find all the answers to the intracacies of pivots.  
j

You are right, we changed the nonlag to show blocks instead of lines, by changing the minimum and maximum values in the common tab to 1 and 2 to straighten the line. I have changed the jpg chart example to reflect this.

  * [#412](/thread/post/4828411#post4828411 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 2, 2011 1:42pm  Aug 2, 2011 1:42pm 

  * [ julie1585](julie1585)

  * | Joined Oct 2009  | Status: Trader | [150 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=118395)

hi,  
  
It doesn't repaint, but as the candle is forming say its going short the current nonlags may turn red but if the candle finishes higher they may turn green. you need to wait for candle close for final colour of last non lag block. it does not repaint older blocks, many people have confirmed.  
  
J

Hi ttaro,  
  
Er well I am sort of using it but encorporating it in my scalping on the EURUSD these days. Using the 5 min to determine direction and trading/scalping the euro in that direction.  
  
  
The system itself if not quite as cut and dry as it was on the Pound as price doesn't pull back to the 20 ema as often on the euro.   
  
I find its most helpful to notice when price pushes through the 20 ema, when it does that on the 5 min a new short term trend is usually forming and it becomes safe to scalp in that direction.  
  
Sorry can't be more helpful as I am not trading the pound at present.

  * Edited 11:05pm  Nov 7, 2011 11:03pm | Edited 11:05pm 

  * [ julie1585](julie1585)

  * | Joined Oct 2009  | Status: Trader | [150 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=118395)

Hi there Highlander,  
  
Yes as far as signals and entries go they look pretty good, but i take a judgement call on closeness to pivots as support or resistance and both those entries although they worked out great this time may have come a cropper on possible pivot bounces.  
  
If there is enough momentum or its news driven it will push through the pivots anyway, but if not you will get some losers that don't follow through if you enter too close to pivots.  
  
PS the 2nd trade I would be less worried about the Ms1 but the first taking it long up into daily pivot can be very risky.  
  
Just my thoguhts on pivots.  
  
J
